+package com.xxx.yyy;

+public final class APNMatchTools
+{
+  public APNMatchTools() {}
+  
+  public static String matchAPN(String paramString)
+  {
+    if (("".equals(paramString)) || (paramString == null)) {
+      return "";
+    }
+    paramString = paramString.toLowerCase();
+    if (paramString.startsWith(APNNet.CMNET)) {

+    }
+    if (paramString.startsWith(APNNet.CMWAP)) {
+      return APNNet.CMWAP;
+    }
+    if (paramString.startsWith(APNNet.GNET_3)) {
+      return APNNet.GNET_3;
+    }
+    if (paramString.startsWith(APNNet.GWAP_3)) {
+      return APNNet.GWAP_3;
+    }
+    if (paramString.startsWith(APNNet.UNINET)) {
+      return APNNet.UNINET;
+    }
+    if (paramString.startsWith(APNNet.UNIWAP)) {
+      return APNNet.UNIWAP;
+    }
+    if (paramString.startsWith("default")) {
+      return "default";
+    }
+    return "";
+  }
+

+  {
+    public static String CMNET;

+    public static String GNET_3;

+    public static String UNIWAP;
+    
+    static
+    {
+      CMNET = "cmnet";
+      GWAP_3 = "3gwap";
+      GNET_3 = "3gnet";
+      UNIWAP = "uniwap";
+    }

+  }
